GYIM SHING KONG JO, RGYA BZA' RJES MA STE, RGYA'I DEB THER LAS,
BOD KYI RGYAL MO KHU DAN GYIS BU MO SLONG DU BYUNG BA LA, RGYA
RJE THANG KRUNG TZUNG GI NU BO YUNG DBANG GI BU MO KIMS SHING
KONG JO BYIN, KENG LUNG GI LO BZHI PA LCAGS KHYI STE SPYI LO 710
LOR BOD KYI ZHANG BTZAN TO RI LHAS BYIN GYIS BSUS, KRUNG TZANG
SKU DNGOS KYIS MGAR CHEN PO ZHING PHENG HYEN GYI BAR DU SKYEL
THUNG RGYA CHER MDZAD DE, MKHAR DE'I NYES PA CAN RNAMS THAR DU
BCUG DMANGS LA KHRAL 'UL LO GCIG MI DGOS PAR BYAS, MKHAR DE'I
MING YANG BRJES TE KONG JO'I MING GYIM SHING ZHES BTAGS, GZHAN
YANG BSTAN BCOS DANG, GOS DAR KHRI TSO DU MA, BZO RIGS DANG SGYU
RTZAL SNA TSOGS PA, ROL MO KHYAD PAR BA CHA TSANG LA SOGS PA
RDZONGS SKAL GYA NOM PA BSTZAL, PHYIS SU SLAR YANG RMA CHU NUB
RGYUD KHUG DGU ZHES PA STE, MI NYAG GI YUL KHAMS THAMS CAD KONG
JO LA BYIN, ZHES DEB DMAR DU ZHIB PAR DRANGS PA LTAR RO, KONG JO
BOD DU BYON NAS KHRI LDE GTZUG BRTAN DANG 'DUS PA LA SRAS KHRI
SRONG LDE BTZAN BYUNG BAS BOD RGYA GNYIS DBON ZHANG DU GYUR,...
